```yaml
            - /url: /gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=TnACMrGVghHocjL8KB&ref_=footer_consumer_health_data_privacy
        - listitem [ref=e4289]:
          - link "Your Ads Privacy Choices" [ref=e4290] [cursor=pointer]:
            - /url: /privacyprefs?ref_=footer_iba
        - listitem [ref=e4291]
      - generic [ref=e4293]: © 1996-2026, Amazon.com, Inc. or its affiliates
```
